SMS System Maintenance Agreement</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Parties:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; width: 100%"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: justify">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in; text-align: right"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in">&#9679;</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Party A (Service Recipient): ALOHA Asia Pacific Limited</TD>
</TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; width: 100%"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: justify">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in; text-align: right"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in">&#9679;</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Party B (Service Provider): Next Technology Holding Inc.</TD>
</TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Date of Signing: Same as the Main Agreement</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Whereas:</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Party A and Party B have signed the &ldquo;Hotel
Monitoring and Management Software NEXT SMS System Development Agreement&rdquo; (hereinafter referred to as the &ldquo;Main Agreement&rdquo;)
regarding the development of the NEXT SMS System for 20 hotels/resorts under Party A. To ensure the long-term stable operation of the
NEXT SMS System &#8212; including the maintenance of SaaS multi-tenant performance and the continuous optimization of AI models &#8212;
both parties agree to sign this &ldquo;Supplementary Maintenance Agreement&rdquo; to clarify the specific content of the maintenance services.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">1. Scope of Maintenance Services</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Party B shall provide annual maintenance services
for the NEXT SMS System deployed in 20 hotels/resorts of Party A, including but not limited to:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">1.1 SaaS Multi-Tenant System Maintenance: Daily
operation monitoring (tenant data isolation, concurrent access stability), vulnerability repair (e.g., tenant login failure), software
version upgrade (compatibility with new PMS systems), tenant-specific configuration adjustment (e.g., adding new user roles for resort
hotels), to ensure the normal operation of the multi-tenant function of the NEXT SMS System.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">1.2 AI Model Maintenance: Quarterly AI model performance
evaluation (using confusion matrix, F1 score), parameter adjustment for drift (e.g., accuracy decrease due to new camera angles), semi-annual
federated learning retraining (using anonymized data from 20 hotels), and optimization of quantized models (adapting to hardware upgrades
of Edge AI Gateways), to ensure that the AI model performance of the NEXT SMS System meets the standards.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">1.3 Edge AI Gateway Maintenance: Monthly firmware
update, debugging of edge AI inference engine (e.g., TensorRT runtime errors), local data backup verification (ensuring no loss of AI
analysis results of the NEXT SMS System).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">1.4 Technical Support: Provide 7&times;24 remote
technical support (phone/email) for general issues, and on-site support within 48 hours for emergency faults (e.g., hardware faults of
Edge AI Gateways, abnormal SaaS multi-tenant data isolation of the NEXT SMS System).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">1.5 Training and Reports: Provide one free training
session per hotel per year (covering AI model performance monitoring of the NEXT SMS System and operation of new SaaS multi- tenant functions), and a monthly maintenance report
(including fault records, AI model accuracy trends, and Edge AI Gateway uptime).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"></P>

    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2. Maintenance Term</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">3 years after the final acceptance date of the
NEXT SMS System (automatically extended if there is no written notice from both parties).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">3. Maintenance Fees and Payment Method</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">3.1 Annual Maintenance Fee: USD 12,000 per hotel/resort
per year. Party A operates a total of 20 hotels/resorts, so the total annual maintenance fee is USD 240,000 (excluding taxes). This fee
includes SaaS multi-tenant maintenance of the NEXT SMS System, AI model retraining, Edge AI Gateway support, and training services.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">3.2 Payment Schedule: A one-time annual transfer
to the designated account of Party B.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">3.3 Payment Method: Same as the Main Agreement
(bank transfer to the designated account of Party B).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">4. Rights and Obligations</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">4.1 Rights and Obligations of Party A:</P>

more than 15 days, a penalty of 0.05% of the outstanding amount shall be charged daily.</TD>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">5. Termination</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>




<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">In the event of a material breach by either party
(e.g., Party A failing to pay maintenance fees for over 30 consecutive days, or Party B failing to resolve the NEXT SMS System AI model
malfunction within 12 hours), the non-breaching party may issue a written notice demanding rectification. If the breaching party fails
to correct the issue within 30 days, the non-breaching party may terminate this agreement and claim compensation for losses (e.g., damages
resulting from prolonged downtime of the NEXT SMS System AI services).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">6. Management law and dispute resolution</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Same as the Main Agreement (subject to the laws
of Hong Kong, disputes shall be settled through arbitration by the Hong Kong International Arbitration Center, which covers NEXT SMS system
AI model maintenance breach compensation and SaaS multi-tenant service quality dispute issues).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Party A (Service Recipient): ALOHA Asia Pacific
Limited</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center">NEXT WATER-ENERGY SYNERGY</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center">Smart Water-Energy Synergy System Development
Contract</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Party A (Employer)</B>: Starlight Garden Limited</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Party B (Developer)</B>: Next Technology Holding
Inc.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Whereas&#65306;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Party A intends to promote water supply pipeline
leakage control, intelligent operation management, and water-energy synergy optimization projects to achieve leakage rate optimization,
operational efficiency improvement, management digitalization, energy consumption reduction, and carbon emission reduction goals.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Party B has the capability of developing the NEXT
WATER-ENERGY SYNERGY Smart Water-Energy Synergy System (hereinafter referred to as the &ldquo;System&rdquo;), integrating equipment, and
implementing projects, which can adapt to carbon peaking/carbon neutrality monitoring, renewable energy access and other needs, and meet
all-dimensional requirements of Party A&rsquo;s project.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">In accordance with the principles of equality,
voluntariness and mutual benefit, and based on international business practices, the two parties hereby enter into this agreement regarding
Party B providing System development and project implementation services to Party A.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Article 1 Project Overview</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">1.1 Project Name</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">NEXT WATER-ENERGY SYNERGY Intelligent Management
and Energy Synergy Optimization Integrated Application Project</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">1.2 Project Goals</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">(1) By the end of 2026, the water supply pipeline
leakage rate &le; 8% (production and sales difference &le; 10%), and the comprehensive energy consumption of water operations reduced
by &ge; 15% compared with that before transformation;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">(2) Establish a full-process System covering &ldquo;perception-platform-dispatching-energy
synergy&rdquo;, realizing real-time collection, correlation analysis and visual management of water and energy data (energy consumption,
PV, carbon emissions);</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">(3) Remote transmission coverage rate of water
meters with DN40 and above &ge; 100%, remote transmission water volume ratio &ge; 95%, energy consumption monitoring coverage rate of
water links &ge; 100%, PV monitoring accuracy &ge; 99% ;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">(4) Establish a &ldquo;water-energy&rdquo; synergy
data security system to ensure the security of pipeline network, user, operation, energy consumption and carbon emission reduction data;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">(5) Annual carbon emission reduction &ge; 50 tons
of CO&#8322;, annual power generation of PV equipment &ge; 100,000 kWh (adapting to microgrid access).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Article 2 Project Content and Scope</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Party B shall complete the following core tasks
to ensure the implementation of the System (including energy synergy module) and the achievement of project goals:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.1 Core Module Development of the System</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; border-collapse: collapse">
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Module Name</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-top: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Content</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Optimized management of infrastructure</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Retain the original pipeline network management function, and add spatial positioning and status monitoring of energy consumption monitoring points (key equipment of water plants and pump stations)</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Marketing optimization management</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Retain the original water sales analysis and production-sales difference calculation functions, and add &ldquo;water volume-energy consumption&rdquo; correlation analysis (e.g., statistics of energy waste caused by leakage)</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Leak control management</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Retain DMA zoned metering and leakage point early warning functions, and add a &ldquo;leakage repair-energy saving&rdquo; calculation model</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Scheduling optimization management</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Combine pressure, flow and water quality data, and add an &ldquo;energy cost-oriented&rdquo; dispatching strategy (e.g., giving priority to high-energy-consuming equipment during PV peak periods)</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Energy optimization management</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#9312; Energy consumption monitoring: real-time collection of voltage/current/power of water plant and pump station equipment (collection frequency &le; 5 minutes/time); &#9313; PV synergy: connect to PV inverters to monitor power generation/grid-connected status (delay &le; 10 seconds); &#9314; Carbon emission reduction accounting: generate daily/monthly/annual emission reduction reports in accordance with ISO 14064</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Optimisation Centre</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Summarize water anomalies (abrupt water volume changes, equipment failures) and energy anomalies (abrupt energy consumption increases, PV power outages), and generate joint optimization suggestions</FONT></TD></TR>
  </TABLE>
<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.2 Construction of Dispatching Command Center</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><I>Hardware Deployment</I>: Add energy monitoring
terminals (energy consumption collectors, PV data receivers) to adapt to the dual-dimensional data processing needs of &ldquo;water + energy&rdquo;.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><I>Software Function</I>: Develop a B/S architecture
visual sub-platform to display real-time energy consumption of each water link, PV power generation and carbon emission reduction progress,
supporting multi-terminal access and hierarchical permission control.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.3 Deployment and Integration of Perception
Layer Equipment</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; border-collapse: collapse">
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Equipment Type</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-top: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Requirements</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Existing water sensing equipment</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Retain flow, pressure and water quality equipment to ensure data accuracy &ge; 99% and breakpoint resume</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Add energy sensing equipment</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#9312; Energy consumption meters: in line with IEC 61850 standard, deployed in distribution boxes; &#9313; PV monitoring equipment: including irradiance sensors (0-2000W/m&sup2;) and inverter data collectors; &#9314; Carbon emission meters: deployed in gas equipment and power access points</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Equipment integration</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Coordinate data collection frequency of energy and water equipment (energy consumption &le; 5 minutes/time, PV &le; 15 minutes/time, carbon emission &le; 1 hour/time)</FONT></TD></TR>
  </TABLE>
<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2.4 Supporting System Construction</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">1. &ldquo;Water-Energy&rdquo; Synergy Data Warehouse:
Add hierarchical modeling of energy data (energy consumption, PV, carbon emissions) to support &ldquo;water volume-energy consumption-carbon
emission&rdquo; correlation analysis.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2. Carbon Emission Reduction Accounting Subsystem:
Build a model in accordance with ISO 14064, automatically capture data and generate internationally certified carbon accounting documents.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">3. Data Security System: Energy consumption, PV
and carbon emission data are transmitted with AES-256 encryption to adapt to the security needs of energy equipment access.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Article 3 Project Cycle</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Total cycle: 18 months, divided into 5 phases&#65306;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; border-collapse: collapse">
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Phase</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-top: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Cycle</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; width: 429px; border-top: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">English Core Work</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Data consolidation</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">1-3 Month</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Refine requirements, collect basic water data, and simultaneously collect Party A&rsquo;s 2-year historical energy consumption data, power grid parameters and PV planning drawings</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Development and procurement</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">4-5 Month</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Develop System software modules (including energy optimization module), purchase water hardware, and simultaneously purchase energy consumption meters and PV monitoring equipment</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Deployment and debugging</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">6-15 Month</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Install water equipment, conduct system integration and joint debugging, and simultaneously complete the installation of energy perception equipment and &ldquo;water-energy&rdquo; data joint debugging</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Test run</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">16-17 Month</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Conduct System trial operation and water operation training, and simultaneously conduct trial operation of energy synergy functions and provide &ge; 2 special trainings on energy optimization</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Acceptance and delivery</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">18 Month</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Conduct System acceptance and deliver results, adding energy-dimensional acceptance (energy consumption reduction rate, carbon emission reduction, PV power generation)</FONT></TD></TR>
  </TABLE>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><I>&nbsp;</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><I>Agreement on Construction Period Delay</I>:
If the delay is caused by Party A&rsquo;s failure to cooperate with PV grid connection, Party B may apply for a construction period extension;
if the delay is caused by Party B&rsquo;s own reasons, Party B shall bear responsibility in accordance with Article 10 of this Contract.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Article 4 Technical Requirements</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">4.1 Applicable Standards</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; border-collapse: collapse">
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Category</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-top: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">English Standards</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Basic standard</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">National/industry standards ISO 9001, IP68</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Special standards for energy</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">IEC 61850 (power system automation), ISO 14064 (greenhouse gas accounting),</FONT></TD></TR>
  </TABLE>
<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">4.2 Key Technical Indicators</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; border-collapse: collapse">
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Indicator Type</FONT></TD>

  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Energy data acquisition</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Energy consumption data loss rate &le; 0.1%, PV data transmission delay &le; 10 seconds, carbon accounting result error rate &le; 2%</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">System response</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Ordinary query of energy module &le; 3 seconds, carbon emission reduction report generation &le; 8 seconds</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Compatibility</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Support connection with Party A&rsquo;s existing power grid system (SCADA), provide API/Web Service interfaces</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Photovoltaic collaboration</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">PV power generation prediction accuracy &ge; 85%, supporting automatic linkage with water dispatching strategies</FONT></TD></TR>
  </TABLE>
<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Article 5 Rights and Obligations of Both
Parties</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">5.1 Rights and Obligations of Party A</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">1. Supervise the development progress of the energy
module and put forward rectification requirements for the accuracy of energy data (rectification period &le; 15 working days); 2. Participate
in the acceptance of delivered energy perception equipment and confirm that the equipment model is consistent with the Contract</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2. Provide basic energy data (historical energy
consumption, power grid access permit, PV site planning drawing) within 20 working days after the Contract takes effect; 2. Coordinate
with the power department to cooperate with PV equipment grid-connected debugging, and provide temporary power supply and network interface
for the PV site; 3. Organize energy-related departments to participate in System acceptance and confirm the carbon emission reduction
and energy consumption reduction rate in accordance with the agreement</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 4 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->4<!-- Field: /Sequence --> / 9</P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">5.2 Rights and Obligations of Party B</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">1. Have the right to apply for cost compensation
if the cost increases due to Party A&rsquo;s failure to provide energy data in a timely manner or cooperate with PV grid connection</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2. Provide original factory qualification certificates
for energy perception equipment (energy consumption meters include MID certification), and the carbon emission reduction module shall
pass the accounting verification of a third party (e.g., SGS); 2. Provide &ge; 2 &ldquo;special trainings on energy optimization&rdquo;
(including energy consumption analysis, carbon accounting, PV dispatching); 3. Bear a 5-year confidentiality responsibility for energy
consumption, carbon emission reduction and PV power generation data; 4. Deliver complete documents of the energy module (energy optimization
manual, carbon accounting algorithm description, PV connection agreement) upon acceptance</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Article 6 Delivery and Acceptance</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">6.1 Acceptance Standards</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; border-collapse: collapse">
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Acceptance Type</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-top: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Standards</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Interim acceptance</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Pass rate of delivered energy perception equipment &ge; 100%, completion rate of energy module development &ge; 100%</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Final acceptance</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">1. Water goal: leakage rate &le; 8%, water meter remote transmission coverage rate &ge; 100%; 2. Energy goal: energy consumption reduction &ge; 15%, annual PV power generation &ge; 100,000 kWh, annual carbon emission reduction &ge; 50 tons of CO&#8322;; 3. System goal: energy data accuracy &ge; 99%, carbon accounting error &le; 2%</FONT></TD></TR>
  </TABLE>
<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">6.2 Acceptance Process</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">1. After completing the phased work, Party B shall
submit the <I>System Acceptance Application</I> and materials (phased work report, test records, equipment certificate).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2. Party A shall organize acceptance within 10
working days after receiving the application, and issue the <I>Phased Acceptance Report</I> if qualified; if unqualified, Party B shall
rectify within 15 working days, and the rectification shall not exceed 2 times.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">3. After the project is fully completed, Party
B shall submit the <I>Final Acceptance Application</I>, and Party A shall organize acceptance within 20 working days and issue the <I>Final
Acceptance Report</I> if qualified.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">4. Dispute Resolution: Disputes related to the
accuracy of energy data and carbon emission reduction accounting shall be evaluated by an internationally recognized institution (e.g.,
SGS, DNV), and the expenses shall be borne by the responsible party.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Article 8 Intellectual Property and Confidentiality</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">8.1 Intellectual Property</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; border-collapse: collapse">
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; width: 16%; border: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Right Owner</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; width: 84%; border-top: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Content</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Party A</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Enjoy permanent right to use the System (including energy module) and ownership of &ldquo;water-energy&rdquo; data generated by the System</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Party B</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Enjoy the software copyright of the System (including energy optimization algorithm, carbon accounting model, PV synergy logic), and the intellectual property rights of jointly developed energy derivative modules belong to Party B</FONT></TD></TR>
  </TABLE>
<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Confidentiality Clause</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">1. Confidential Scope: Including but not limited
to Party A&rsquo;s energy consumption data, carbon emission reduction data, PV power generation data, and Party B&rsquo;s System algorithms
and technical documents.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2. Confidentiality Period: The confidentiality
period for energy consumption, carbon emission reduction and PV power generation data is 5 years, and the confidentiality period for other
trade secrets is 3 years after the Contract is terminated.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">3. Liability for Breach: Any party that discloses
confidential information shall pay a penalty of 20% of the total contract amount (USD 1,440,000.00) and compensate the other party for
direct losses.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Article 9 Liability for Breach</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">9.1 Party A&rsquo;s Liability for Breach</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; border-collapse: collapse">
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Breach Scenario</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-top: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Liability</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Overdue payment</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Pay a penalty of 0.05% of the overdue amount per day; if overdue for more than 60 days, Party B has the right to suspend System development, and Party A shall compensate Party B for 120% of the invested cost</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Failure to provide energy data or cooperate with photovoltaic grid connection</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Compensate Party B for additional costs incurred due to waiting for data and on-site coordination</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Unauthorized transfer of systems or secondary development</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Pay a penalty of 5% of the total contract amount (USD 360,000.00)</FONT></TD></TR>
  </TABLE>
<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">9.2 Party B&rsquo;s Liability for Breach</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; border-collapse: collapse">
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="border: Black 1pt solid; padding: 5pt">
    <P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center">Breach Scenario</P></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-top: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Liability</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Overdue delivery systems</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Pay a penalty of 0.05% of the total contract amount (USD 3,600.00) per day; if overdue for more than 60 days, Party A has the right to terminate the Contract, and Party B shall refund the received payment and compensate for losses</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">The energy module is not up to standard (e.g. carbon accounting error exceeds 2%)</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Pay a penalty of 5% of the total contract amount (USD 360,000.00) and rectify within 15 working days</FONT></TD></TR>
  <TR>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; border-right: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-left: Black 1pt solid; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">More than 48 hours of maintenance for faults during the warranty period of photovoltaic equipment (excluding extended business trip)</FONT></TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 5pt; vertical-align: top; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid; border-right: Black 1pt solid; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Pay a penalty of USD 10,000.00 per occurrence</FONT></TD></TR>
  </TABLE>
<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Article 10 Force Majeure</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">1. Scope of Force Majeure: Including earthquakes,
wars, cross-border logistics interruptions, policy adjustments between China and the US leading to obstacles in System development or
equipment import, as well as power system failures (not caused by Party A), PV module supply chain interruptions, and carbon accounting
standard policy adjustments.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2. Notification Obligation: The affected party
shall notify the other party in writing within 24 hours and provide supporting materials (e.g., logistics interruption notice, policy
document) within 7 working days.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">3. Exemption from Liability: If the Contract cannot
be performed due to force majeure, the two parties shall negotiate to terminate the Contract, and the incurred expenses shall be settled
according to the actual workload; if part of the Contract can be performed, the two parties shall negotiate to extend the construction
period.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Article 11 Dispute Resolution</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">1. Disputes shall first be resolved through friendly
negotiation (negotiation period: 30 days).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2. If negotiation fails, either party has the
right to file a lawsuit with the competent court at the place where Party B is located, or submit the dispute to the American Arbitration
Association (AAA) for arbitration in accordance with its international arbitration rules (arbitration place: New York, arbitration tribunal
composed of 3 members).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">3. During the dispute period, except for the disputed
matters, the other clauses of the Contract and the development and delivery of the undisputed part of the System shall continue to be
performed.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"></P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Article 12 Miscellaneous</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">1. Contract Modification: Adjustments to the energy
module function or changes to the PV equipment model shall be confirmed in writing by both parties, and the supplementary agreement shall
have the same legal effect as this Contract.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">2. Contract Effectiveness: This Contract shall
take effect from the date of signature and seal by both parties.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">3. Number of Contract Copies: This Contract is
made in 6 copies, with 3 copies held by each party, all having the same legal effect.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

and mutual benefit, in accordance with the Original Contract and relevant laws and international business practices.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.25in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.25in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Article 1 Definition of Core Terms</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in">1.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>System</B>: Refers to the integrated system delivered by Party B under
the Original Contract, including but not limited to 6 core modules (infrastructure optimization management, marketing optimization management,
leak control management, scheduling optimization management, energy optimization management, Optimization Centre), perception-layer equipment
(existing water sensing equipment, energy consumption meters, PV monitoring equipment, carbon emission meters) and the dispatching command
center (hardware terminals + B/S architecture visual sub-platform).</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.25in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.25in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in">2.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>Maintenance Services</B>: Refers to the exclusive services provided by
Party B to Party A under this Agreement, including daily operation monitoring, fault diagnosis and repair, system version optimization,
data security maintenance, technical training and other services as specified in Article 3.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.25in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.25in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in">3.</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt"><B>Critical Fault</B>: Refers to faults that cause the System to stop operating
(e.g., PV monitoring data interruption for more than 2 hours, carbon accounting subsystem failure, large-area water leakage early warning
function failure) and affect Party A&rsquo;s normal water supply management or energy synergy business.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.25in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.25in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.25in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.25in"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1; Options: NewSection -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->1<!-- Field: /Sequence --> / 7</P></DIV>
